<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 2.02&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Results of
Operations and Financial Condition</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On October 13, 2004, Apple Computer,&nbsp;Inc. (Apple) issued a press
release regarding Apple&#146;s financial results for its fourth fiscal quarter ended
September 25, 2004 and a related data sheet. A copy of Apple&#146;s press release is
attached hereto as Exhibit&nbsp;99.1 and a copy of the related data sheet is
attached hereto as Exhibit&nbsp;99.2.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The information contained in this Current Report shall not be deemed
&#147;filed&#148; for purposes of Section 18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as
amended (the Exchange Act), or incorporated by reference in any filing under
the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as shall be
expressly set forth by specific reference in such a filing.</font></p>

<body lang="EN-US">

<div>

<p align="right" style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit 99.1</font></b></p>

<p align="right" style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple Reports Fourth
Quarter Results</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Revenue Increases 37
Percent Year-Over-Year</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">iPod Shipments Top 2
million</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">CUPERTINO,
California&#151;October 13, 2004&#151;Apple&#174; today announced financial results for its
fiscal 2004 fourth quarter ended September 25, 2004. For the quarter, the
Company posted a net profit of $106 million, or $.26 per diluted share. These
results compare to a net profit of $44 million, or $.12 per diluted share, in
the year-ago quarter. Revenue for the quarter was $2.35 billion, up 37 percent
from the year-ago quarter. Gross margin was 27.0 percent, up from 26.6 percent
in the year-ago quarter. International sales accounted for 37 percent of the
quarter&#146;s revenue.</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The quarter&#146;s results
include an after-tax restructuring charge of $4 million. Excluding this charge,
the Company&#146;s net profit for the quarter would have been $110 million, or $.27
per diluted share.</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple shipped 836,000
Macintosh&#174; units and 2,016,000 iPods during the quarter, representing a 6
percent increase in CPU units and a 500 percent increase in iPods over the
year-ago quarter.</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;We are thrilled to
report our highest fourth quarter revenue in nine years,&#148; said Steve Jobs,
Apple&#146;s CEO. &#147;We shipped over 2 million iPods, our Retail store revenue grew 95
percent year-over-year, and the new iMac G5 has received phenomenal reviews and
is off to a great start.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;We&#146;re pleased to report
37 percent revenue growth for the quarter and operating margin above 5
percent,&#148; said Peter Oppenheimer, Apple&#146;s CFO. &#147;Looking ahead to the first
quarter of fiscal 2005, we expect revenue of between $2.8 and $2.9 billion,
operating margin above 7 percent and earnings per diluted share of $.39 to
$.42.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the year, the Company
reported net income of $276 million on revenue of $8.28 billion compared to net
income of $69 million on revenue of $6.21 billion in 2003.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>


<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\nogwal\04-11506-1\task196195\11506-1-mm.htm',USER='nogwal',CD='Oct 13 10:42 2004' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<p align="center" style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Non-GAAP Measures</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company believes that
presentation of results excluding items such as restructuring charges and
investment gains provides meaningful supplemental information to both
management and investors that is indicative of the Company&#146;s core operating
results and facilitates comparison of operating results across reporting
periods. The Company includes a full income statement reconciliation of these
non-GAAP measures to provide a more complete view of their effect on results.</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple will provide live
streaming of its Q4 2004 financial results conference call utilizing
QuickTime&#153;, Apple&#146;s standards-based technology for live and on-demand audio and
video streaming. The live webcast will begin at 2:00 p.m. PDT on Wednesday,
October 13, 2004 at http://www.apple.com/quicktime/qtv/earningsq404/ and will
also be available for replay. The QuickTime player is available free for
Macintosh and Windows users at www.apple.com/quicktime.</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This press release
contains forward-looking statements about the Company&#146;s estimated revenue and
earnings for the first quarter of fiscal 2005. These statements involve risks
and uncertainties and actual results may differ. Potential risks and
uncertainties include continued competitive pressures in the marketplace; the
effect competitive and economic factors and the Company&#146;s reaction to them may
have on consumer and business buying decisions with respect to the Company&#146;s
products; the ability of the Company to make timely delivery of new programs,
products and successful technological innovations to the marketplace; the
continued availability of certain components and services essential to the
Company&#146;s business currently obtained by the Company from sole or limited
sources, including the timely resolution of manufacturing issues associated
with the G5 microprocessors used in many of the Company&#146;s Macintosh systems;
possible disruption in commercial activities caused by terrorist activity and
armed conflict, such as changes in logistics and security arrangements, and
reduced end-user purchases relative to expectations; possible disruption in
commercial activity as a result of major health concerns including epidemics;
risks associated with the Company&#146;s retail initiative including significant
investment cost, uncertain consumer acceptance and potential impact on existing
reseller relationships; the effect that the Company&#146;s dependency on
manufacturing and logistics services provided by third-parties may have on the
quality, quantity or cost of products manufactured or services rendered; the
Company&#146;s reliance on the availability of third-party music content, and the
ability of the Company to successfully evolve its operating system and attract
sufficient Macintosh developers. More information on potential factors that
could affect the Company&#146;s financial results is included from time to time in
the Company&#146;s public reports filed with the SEC, including the Company&#146;s Forms
10-Q for the quarters ended December 27, 2003, March 27, 2004 and June 26,
2004; and the </font></p>

<p align="center" style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<p align="center" style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Company&#146;s
Form 10-K for the 2004 fiscal year to be filed with the SEC. The Company
assumes no obligation to update any forward-looking statements or information,
which speak as of their respective dates.</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple ignited the
personal computer revolution in the 1970s with the Apple II and reinvented the
personal computer in the 1980s with the Macintosh. Today, Apple continues to
lead the industry in innovation with its award-winning desktop and notebook
computers, OS X operating system, and iLife and professional applications.
Apple is also spearheading the digital music revolution with its iPod portable
music players and iTunes online music store.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="line-height:11.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">UNAUDITED
CONDENSED CONSOLIDATED STATEMENTS OF OPERATIONS</font></p>

<p align="center" style="line-height:11.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="line-height:11.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(In millions,
except share and per share amounts)</font></p>

<p align="center" style="line-height:11.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="100%" style="border-collapse:collapse;width:100.0%;">
 <tr style="page-break-inside:avoid;">
  <td width="43%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:43.02%;">
  <p style="line-height:11.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">

<p align="right" style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit 99.2</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Apple Computer, Inc.</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Q404 Unaudited Summary Data</font></b></p>
